 logon ke man menonline shoppingko lekar kai tarah kii ashankaayen rahati hai
 These fears are and should be related to online fraud, which is a huge boom in online fraud cases nowadays
 vaise bhi aap jis vyakti yavebsitepar bharosa karke product kharid rahe hai, use sidhe taur par to jaanate nahin hai
 He has a virtual identity with which you are aware
 aise main aap sochenge ki'cash on delivery'behatar vikalp he
 But even in the case of 'cash on delivery', you pay the price without seeing the product you purchased
 yani aap uski panking dekhakar paise de dete hai
 In such a situation, how can you minimize your risk in online shopping and how can you avoid such fraud
 yahaan jaaniye kuch upaay
 
 
 1
 oficial celler se khariden samacemejan or flipcart jaisi i-commers websites duniyabar ke vikritaon ko market place muhaiyaa karaati hai, ye website swayan koi product nahin bechati hai
 While not all sellers on these websites are the same, there are some vendors who can be considered almost 'official sellers' of these e-commerce websites
 flipcart ke maamle main yah darja 'dablyooes retail' ko hasil he
 That is, buying from this seller on Flipkart is 100 percent safe
 haalanki isi website par maujuud anya vikritaon ke mukaable 'dablyooes retail' par keemten thodi zyada ho sakati hai, lekin laalach naa karen
 Not only this, 'WS Retail' is the only seller on Flipkart that offers a 30-day money back guarantee, while the rest of the sellers offer a 7 to 10-day return guarantee
 amejan par yah darja 'cloudtail' ko hasil he
 Most products on Jabong and Myntra are sold by official vendors
 haalanki yahaan bhi third party vikreta maujuud hai, lekin koshish karen ki aap sidhe mintra yaa jabong se apni manapsand cheez khariden
 And yes, official sellers also take less shipping time
 2
 Buy similar products that are in the warehouse E-commerce websites like Amazon, Flipkart and Snapdeal have their own warehouse, where third party vendors also have their goods
 pehle se godaam main maujuud saamaan ko agar aap kharidte hai to phir inaki shipping third party vikreta nahin balki vah website swayan karti he, jisase aapane kharida he
 If you want to know whether the product you are buying is present in the warehouse or not, then tell us that such products are tagged with 'amazon Fulfilled' on Amazon, 'flipkart Advantage' on Flipkart and 'safeship' on Snapdee
 
 3
 Look at the seller's rating too
 Before you press the Buy button to buy the product of your choice, be sure to check the seller's rating
 khaastaur par ibe or snapdil jaisi websiton ke maamle main yah jarur karen
 Keep in mind that only buy goods from sellers who have done at least 50 or more transactions and their rating is also 90 percent or at least 4 stars
 jitani zyada reating hogi utana hi zyada aap us vikreta par bharosa kar sakate hai
 4
 ibe par karen shopping ko 'paisaape' se hi karen bhugtanhaalanki 'cash on delivery' ko kaaphi surakshit mana jaataa he, lekin yah utani bhi zyada surakshit nahin he jitna samajha jaataa he
 Especially not in the case of ebay transactions
 ibe par agar aap 'paisaape' ke jariye bhugtan karke product kharidte hai to yah website tab tak vikreta ko bhugtan nahin karti he, jab tak product aapke haath main naa aa jaae or aap usase santusht naa ho jaaen
 After receiving the product, ebay stops the money as soon as you receive your complaint and tries to solve your problem
 agar aap product se khush nahin hai to ibe aapke rupee lautaa detaa he
 But, let us know that ebay will not help you in the case of 'cash on delivery'
 5
 Don't get caught in the cheap and discount affair, if you are getting an expensive product on a shopping website very cheap and if you are planning to buy it, then stop
 kyonki is tarah se aapako saste kaa jhansa dekar aapaki mehnat kii kamai udaane waalon kii bhi koi kami nahin he
 Many times it has also been seen that things like stone, plastic or soap are delivered to the giftpack by giving customers the temptation to give expensive things cheaply
 aisa bhi nahin he ki online shopping main mahangi chizon par discount dekar unhen saste main nahin bechaa jaataa, lekin jab bhi aisi deal par clic karen to hameshaa dhyaan rakhen ki aap aadhikarik vikreta se hi khariddaari karen
 Many times you will see that the seller has got good ratings, but he has done only 18-20 transactions so far, so avoid trusting such seller
